Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Luminary 97, the original release of the Apollo 11 Lunar Module (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with source code of Luminary 99 revision 1 previously transcribed from a digitized copy of that program. The code was then updated by undoing changes described in original Luminary memos 83 and 85, using asterisks indicating changed lines in the listing as a guide. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021152D. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Luminary 099 revision 001 printout, although the added code would likely have changed page numbers for a real Luminary 97 listing.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository.

016100,000006:                                                                                                  ##              original release of the flight software for the Lunar 
016101,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 11.
016102,000008:                                                                                                  ##              The code has been recreated from a copy of Luminary 99
016103,000009:                                                                                                  ##              revision 001, using asterisks indicating changed lines in
016104,000010:                                                                                                  ##              the listing and Luminary Memos #83 and #85, which list 
016105,000011:                                                                                                  ##              changes between Luminary 97 and 98, and 98 and 99. The
016106,000012:                                                                                                  ##              code has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
016107,000013:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Luminary 97 in NASA drawing
016108,000014:                                                                                                  ##              2021152D, which gives relatively high confidence that the
016109,000015:                                                                                                  ##              reconstruction is correct.

016117,000023:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016118,000024:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
016119,000025:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
016120,000026:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
016121,000027: 
016122,000028:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
016123,000029: 
016124,000030:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
016125,000031:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
016126,000032:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
016127,000033:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
016128,000034: 
016129,000035:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
016130,000036:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
016131,000037:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
016132,000038:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
016133,000039:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
016134,000040: 
016135,000041:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
016136,000042:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
016137,000043:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
016138,000044:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
016139,000045: 
016140,000046:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
016141,000047:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
016142,000048:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016177,000083: 
016178,000084:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES -
016179,000085: 
016180,000086:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
016181,000087:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
016182,000088:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
016183,000089:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
016184,000090:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016185,000091: 
016186,000092:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
016187,000093:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
016188,000094:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
016189,000095:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
016190,000096: 
016191,000097:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
016192,000098:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
016193,000099:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
016194,000100:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
016195,000101:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016196,000102: 
016197,000103:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
016198,000104: 
016199,000105:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
016200,000106:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
016201,000107:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 391 

016203,000109:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
016204,000110:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
016205,000111:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
016206,000112:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
016207,000113:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
016208,000114:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
016209,000115:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
016210,000116:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
016211,000117:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
016212,000118:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
016213,000119: 
016214,000120:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
016215,000121:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
016216,000122:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
016217,000123: 
016218,000124:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
016219,000125: 
016220,000126:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
016221,000127:                                                                                                  #        IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
016222,000128:                                                                                                  #        ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
016223,000129: 
016224,000130:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
016225,000131:                                                                                                  #        IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
016226,000132:                                                                                                  #        (WITH OCTAL 01501).
016227,000133:                                                                                                  #        IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
016228,000134:                                                                                                  #        CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
016229,000135:                                                                                                  #                1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
016230,000136:                                                                                                  #                2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
016231,000137: 
016232,000138:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
016233,000139:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016234,000140: 
016235,000141:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
016236,000142: 
016237,000143:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
016238,000144:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL). :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
016239,000145:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
016240,000146:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
016241,000147: 
016242,000148:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION -
016243,000149: 
016244,000150:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
016245,000151:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
016246,000152:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
016247,000153:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
016248,000154: 
016249,000155:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 392 

016251,000157:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
016252,000158: 
016253,000159:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST -
016254,000160: 
016255,000161:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
016256,000162:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
016257,000163: 
016258,000164:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
016259,000165:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
016260,000166:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
016261,000167:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
016262,000168: 
016263,000169:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
016264,000170:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
016265,000171: 
016266,000172:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
016267,000173:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
016268,000174:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
016269,000175:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
016270,000176: 
016271,000177:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
016272,000178:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
016273,000179: 
016274,000180:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
016275,000181:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
016276,000182: 
016277,000183:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
016278,000184: 
016279,000185:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
016280,000186:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
016281,000187:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
016282,000188:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016283,000189: 
016284,000190:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
016285,000191:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
016286,000192: 
016287,000193:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
016288,000194:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
016289,000195: 
016290,000196:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
016291,000197:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
016292,000198:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
016293,000199:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

016418,000324:                                                                                                  #  NNADTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
016419,000325:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
016420,000326:                                                                                                  #  IDAD1TEM      ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
016421,000327:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.

016423,000329:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.

016425,000331:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.

016427,000333:

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

016471,000377: 
016472,000378:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
016473,000379:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
016474,000380:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
016475,000381:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
016476,000382:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
016477,000383:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
016478,000384: 
016479,000385:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
016480,000386:                                                                                                  #  MD1   MD2                             (MAJOR MODE)
016481,000387:                                                                                                  #  VD1   VD2 (VERB)      ND1     ND2     (NOUN)
016482,000388:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  R1D2    R1D3    R1D4    R1D5    (R1)
016483,000389:                                                                                                  #  R2D1  R2D2    R2D3    R2D4    R2D5    (R2)
016484,000390:                                                                                                  #  R3D1  R3D2    R3D3    R3D4    R3D5    (R3)
016485,000391: 
016486,000392:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
016487,000393: 
016488,000394:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
016489,000395:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24              R2D2    10
016490,000396:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23              R2D3     7
016491,000397:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22              R2D4     6
016492,000398:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21              R2D5     5
016493,000399:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20              R3D1     4
016494,000400:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16              R3D2     3
016495,000401:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15              R3D3     2
016496,000402:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14              R3D4     1
016497,000403:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13              R3D5     0
016498,000404:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
016499,000405: 
016500,000406:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
016501,000407: 
016502,000408:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB                RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
016503,000409:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
016504,000410:                                                                                                  #  10            1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2 (24)
016505,000411:                                                                                                  #  9             1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2 (22)
016506,000412:                                                                                                  #  8             1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2 (20)
016507,000413:                                                                                                  #  7             1000                                            R1D1 (16)

Page 397 

016509,000415:                                                                                                  #  6             0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
016510,000416:                                                                                                  #  5             0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
016511,000417:                                                                                                  #  4             0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
016512,000418:                                                                                                  #  3             0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
016513,000419:                                                                                                  #  2             0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
016514,000420:                                                                                                  #  1             0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
016515,000421:                                                                                                  #  0             0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
016516,000422:                                                                                                  #                0000        NO RELAYWORD
016517,000423: 
016518,000424:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
016519,000425: 
016520,000426:                                                                                                  #  BLANK 00000
016521,000427:                                                                                                  #  0     10101
016522,000428:                                                                                                  #  1     00011
016523,000429:                                                                                                  #  2     11001
016524,000430:                                                                                                  #  3     11011
016525,000431:                                                                                                  #  4     01111
016526,000432:                                                                                                  #  5     11110
016527,000433:                                                                                                  #  6     11100
016528,000434:                                                                                                  #  7     10011
016529,000435:                                                                                                  #  8     11101
016530,000436:                                                                                                  #  9     11111
016531,000437: 
016532,000438:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
016533,000439: 
016534,000440:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
016535,000441:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016536,000442:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11

016939,000845:                                                                                                  #  DATA. THE SIGN OF REQRET DETERMINES THE PASS, + FOR PASS 0, - FOR HIGHER
016940,000846:                                                                                                  #  PASSES.

017227,001133:

Page 413 

017229,001135:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
017230,001136: 
017231,001137:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
017232,001138:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
017233,001139:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
017234,001140:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
017235,001141:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
017236,001142: 
017237,001143:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
017238,001144:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
017239,001145: 
017240,001146:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
017241,001147: 
017242,001148:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
017243,001149:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
017244,001150:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
017245,001151: 
017246,001152:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
017247,001153:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
017248,001154:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017249,001155:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
017250,001156:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
017251,001157:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
017252,001158: 
017253,001159:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
017254,001160:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
017255,001161:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
017256,001162:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
017257,001163:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
017258,001164: 
017259,001165:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
017260,001166:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
017261,001167: 
017262,001168:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
017263,001169: 
017264,001170:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
017265,001171:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
017266,001172:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017267,001173:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
017268,001174:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
017269,001175: 
017270,001176:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
017271,001177:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
017272,001178:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
017273,001179: 
017274,001180:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
017275,001181:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
017276,001182: 
017277,001183:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
017278,001184:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
017279,001185:

Page 414 

017281,001187:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
017282,001188: 
017283,001189: 41,2353           44752        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
017284,001190: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST

018392,002298:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
018393,002299:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
018394,002300:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
018395,002301:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
018396,002302:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
018397,002303: 
018398,002304:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
018399,002305:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
018400,002306:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
018401,002307:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
018402,002308:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
018403,002309:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
018404,002310:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
018405,002311: 
018406,002312:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
018407,002313:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018408,002314:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
018409,002315: 
018410,002316:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
018411,002317:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
018412,002318: 
018413,002319:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
018414,002320:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
018415,002321: 
018416,002322:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

018542,002448:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
018543,002449:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
018544,002450:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
018545,002451:                                                                                                  #  
018546,002452:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
018547,002453: 
018548,002454:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
018549,002455:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
018550,002456:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
018551,002457: 
018552,002458:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
018553,002459:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
018554,002460:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
018555,002461: 
018556,002462: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
018557,002463: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
018558,002464: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
018559,002465: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
018560,002466: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
018561,002467: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
018562,002468: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
018563,002469: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

Page 450 

018980,002886: 
018981,002887:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
018982,002888: 
018983,002889:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
018984,002890: 
018985,002891:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
018986,002892:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
018987,002893:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
018988,002894:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
018989,002895: 
018990,002896:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
018991,002897:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
018992,002898:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
018993,002899: 
018994,002900:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
018995,002901:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
018996,002902:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
018997,002903:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
018998,002904:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
018999,002905:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
019000,002906:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
019001,002907:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
019002,002908:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST. THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
019003,002909:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
019004,002910:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
019005,002911: 
019006,002912: 40,3461           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
019007,002913: 40,3462           00006                           EXTEND                                         
019008,002914: 40,3463           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
019009,002915: 40,3464           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
019010,002916: 40,3465           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019011,002917: 40,3466           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
019012,002918: 40,3467           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019013,002919: 40,3470           03477                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
019014,002920: 40,3471           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
019015,002921: 40,3472           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
019016,002922: 40,3473           03475                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
019017,002923: 40,3474           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019018,002924: 40,3475           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
019019,002925: 40,3476           21050                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
019020,002926: 40,3477           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
019021,002927: 40,3500           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
019022,002928: 40,3501           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
019023,002929: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
019024,002930: 40,3503           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
019025,002931: 40,3504           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019026,002932: 
019027,002933: 40,3505                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
019028,002934:

Page 451 

019030,002936:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
019031,002937:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
019032,002938:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
019033,002939:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
019034,002940:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
019035,002941: 
019036,002942:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
019037,002943:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS -
019038,002944:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
019039,002945: 
019040,002946:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
019041,002947:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
019042,002948: 
019043,002949:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019044,002950:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
019045,002951:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
019046,002952:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
019047,002953:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
019048,002954: 
019049,002955:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
019050,002956:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
019051,002957:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
019052,002958:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
019053,002959: 
019054,002960:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
019055,002961:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
019056,002962:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
019057,002963:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
019058,002964:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
019059,002965:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
019060,002966:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
019061,002967: 
019062,002968:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
019063,002969:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
019064,002970: 
019065,002971:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
019066,002972:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
019067,002973: 
019068,002974:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
019069,002975:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
019070,002976: 
019071,002977:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
019072,002978:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
019073,002979:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
019074,002980:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
019075,002981:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
019076,002982:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
019077,002983:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
019078,002984: 
019079,002985:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 452 

019081,002987:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
019082,002988:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
019083,002989:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
019084,002990:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
019085,002991:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
019086,002992:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
019087,002993:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
019088,002994:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
019089,002995:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
019090,002996: 
019091,002997:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
019092,002998:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
019093,002999:

019205,003111:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
019206,003112:    4204           34735        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
019207,003113:    4205           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
019208,003114:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
019209,003115:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019210,003116: 
019211,003117:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
019212,003118:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019213,003119:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
019214,003120:                                                                                                  #                -0              DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
019215,003121:                                                                                                  #                        OR      RESEQUENCE      SET BY VERB 32
019216,003122: 
019217,003123:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
019218,003124:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
019219,003125:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
019220,003126:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019221,003127:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019222,003128:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
019223,003129:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
019224,003130:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
019225,003131:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
019226,003132:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
019227,003133: 
019228,003134:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 455 

019230,003136:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
019231,003137:                                                                                                  #  1)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
019232,003138:                                                                                                  #        EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019233,003139:                                                                                                  #  2)    DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
019234,003140:                                                                                                  #        NVSUBUSY.
019235,003141: 
019236,003142:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
019237,003143:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
019238,003144:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
019239,003145:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
019240,003146:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
019241,003147:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
019242,003148:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
019243,003149:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019244,003150: 
019245,003151:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
019246,003152: 
019247,003153:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019248,003154:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
019249,003155:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
019250,003156:    4223           04227                           TC       DSPABORT

019395,003301:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED), TERMINATE VERB IS EXECUTED, OR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA VERB IS
019396,003302:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IT WAKES UP JOB THAT DID TC ENDIDLE.

019398,003304:                                                                                                  #  IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0, IT PUTS +0 INTO DSPLOCK, AND TURNS OFF KEY RLSE
019399,003305:                                                                                                  #  LIGHT IF DSPLIST IS EMPTY (LEAVES KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF NOT EMPTY).
