019574,003480:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
019575,003481: 
019576,003482:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
019577,003483:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
019578,003484:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
019579,003485:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
019580,003486: 
019581,003487:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019582,003488:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1) BY ENDIDLE
019583,003489:                                                                                                  #                2) BY NVSUBUSY
019584,003490:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
019585,003491:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019586,003492:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
019587,003493:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
019588,003494: 
019589,003495:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
019590,003496:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
019591,003497:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
019592,003498:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
019593,003499:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
019594,003500: 
019595,003501:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
019596,003502:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
019597,003503:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
019598,003504:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
019599,003505:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
019600,003506: 
019601,003507:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
019602,003508:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
019603,003509:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
019604,003510: 
019605,003511: 
019606,003512:                                                                                                  #  .
019607,003513: 
019608,003514:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
019609,003515:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
019610,003516:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
019611,003517:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
019612,003518: 
019613,003519:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
019614,003520:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
019615,003521:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
019616,003522:                                                                                                  #  1)    DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
019617,003523:                                                                                                  #        IS EXCEEDED.
019618,003524:                                                                                                  #  2)    CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 464 

019620,003526:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
019621,003527: 
019622,003528:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
019623,003529:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
019624,003530:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
019625,003531:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
019626,003532:    4443           10647                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
019627,003533:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
019628,003534: 
019629,003535:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
019630,003536:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
019631,003537: 
019632,003538: 04,2647                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
019633,003539: 04,2647                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019634,003540: 04,2647           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
019635,003541: 04,2650           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
019636,003542: 04,2651           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
019637,003543: 04,2652           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
019638,003544: 04,2653           30001                           CA       L                                     
019639,003545: 04,2654           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
019640,003546: 04,2655           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
019641,003547: 
019642,003548:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
019643,003549:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
019644,003550:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
019645,003551:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
019646,003552:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
019647,003553: 
019648,003554:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
019649,003555:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
019650,003556:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
019651,003557:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
019652,003558:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
019653,003559:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019654,003560:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
019655,003561:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
019656,003562:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
019657,003563:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
019658,003564:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
019659,003565:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
019660,003566:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
019661,003567: 
019662,003568:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
019663,003569:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
019664,003570:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
019665,003571: 
019666,003572:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
019667,003573:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
019668,003574:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

Page 465 

019670,003576:    4462           00004                           INHINT                                         
019671,003577:    4463           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
019672,003578:    4464           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
019673,003579:    4465           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
019674,003580:    4466           04470                           TC       +2                                    
019675,003581:    4467           04473                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
019676,003582:    4470           34755                           CAF      ZERO

019681,003587:    4475           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)
019682,003588:    4476           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT

019688,003594:                                                                                                  #  EMPTY. LEAVE KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF 
019689,003595:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST IS NOT EMPTY.

019693,003599:    4507           34755                           CAF      ZERO                                  #  -  NOT EMPTY. LEAVE KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE

019700,003606:                                                                                                  #  PINTEST IS NEEDED FOR AUTO CHECK OF PINBALL.

019810,003716:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
019811,003717:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
019812,003718:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
019813,003719:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
019814,003720:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
019815,003721:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
019816,003722:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
019817,003723:

019819,003725: 40,3603                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

019821,003727: 40,3604           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #  LIGHT RESET LEAVES DSPLOCK UNCHANGED.

019825,003731: 40,3610           05011                           WOR      DSALMOUT                              #  BIT10 CHAN 11

019827,003733: 40,3612           71036                           MASK     DSPTAB     +11D                       #  TURNING OFF AUTO, HOLD, FREE,

019832,003738: 40,3617           65026                           AD       PRIO16                                #  EXISTS, THE ALARM WILL COME BACK.
